{% if result and matrix %}
  <div class="card">
    <header class="page-header-block">
      <h2 class="page-title">Scan results</h2>
      <p class="page-description">
        Matrix of files versus sources. Use <strong>Compare</strong> for file detail and diffs;
        <strong>Set Gold</strong> when you need a fixed source of truth for a path.
      </p>
    </header>
    <p><strong>Scan ID:</strong> {{ result.scan_id }}</p>
    <p><strong>Domain:</strong> {{ result.domain_id }}</p>
    <p><strong>Path filter:</strong> {{ result.path_input or "None" }}</p>
    <p><strong>Sources:</strong> {{ result.source_ids | join(", ") }}</p>

    {% if result.warnings %}
      <div class="warning">
        <strong>Warnings:</strong>
        <ul>
          {% for warning in result.warnings %}
            <li>{{ warning }}</li>
          {% endfor %}
        </ul>
      </div>
    {% endif %}

    <div class="matrix-help">
      <p class="matrix-legend-title">Cell colors</p>
      <ul class="matrix-legend" aria-label="Matrix cell color legend">
        <li>
          <span class="legend-swatch legend-swatch-green" aria-hidden="true"></span>
          Green = identical to baseline
        </li>
        <li>
          <span class="legend-swatch legend-swatch-orange" aria-hidden="true"></span>
          Orange = small difference
        </li>
        <li>
          <span class="legend-swatch legend-swatch-red" aria-hidden="true"></span>
          Red = large difference
        </li>
        <li class="matrix-legend-variants">
          V1 / V2 / V3 = different content variants
        </li>
      </ul>
      <p
        class="matrix-variant-note"
        title="Variants represent identical content groups (same checksum)"
      >
        Variants represent identical content groups (same checksum).
      </p>
    </div>

    <div class="matrix-scroll">
      <table class="matrix">
        <thead>
          <tr>
            <th class="col-file">File</th>
            {% for src in matrix.sources %}
              <th class="col-source" title="{{ src.name }} ({{ src.id }})">{{ src.name }}</th>
            {% endfor %}
            <th
              class="col-gold"
              title="Manual gold only: persisted in data/gold/gold_decisions.json"
            >Gold</th>
            <th class="col-baseline">Baseline</th>
            <th class="col-baseline-type">Baseline Type</th>
            <th class="col-status">Status</th>
            <th class="col-actions">Actions</th>
          </tr>
        </thead>
        <tbody>
          {% for row in matrix.rows %}
            <tr class="status-{{ row.status.lower() }}">
              <td class="col-file"><code>{{ row.relative_path }}</code></td>
              {% for src in matrix.sources %}
                <td class="matrix-cell bucket-{{ row.cells[src.id].bucket }}">
                  {% if row.cells[src.id].missing %}
                    <span class="cell-variant">-</span>
                    <span class="cell-score">-</span>
                  {% else %}
                    <span
                      class="cell-variant"
                      title="Variants represent identical content groups (same checksum)"
                    >{{ row.cells[src.id].variant_label }}</span>
                    <span class="cell-score">{{ row.cells[src.id].score_display }}</span>
                  {% endif %}
                </td>
              {% endfor %}
              <td class="col-gold">{{ row.gold_display }}</td>
              <td class="col-baseline">
                {% if row.baseline_kind == 'GOLD' %}
                  <span class="baseline-prefix baseline-prefix-gold">GOLD:</span>
                  {{ row.baseline_display }}
                {% else %}
                  <span class="baseline-prefix baseline-prefix-suggested">Suggested:</span>
                  {{ row.baseline_display }}
                {% endif %}
              </td>
              <td class="col-baseline-type">{{ row.baseline_kind }}</td>
              <td class="col-status">{{ row.status }}</td>
              <td class="col-actions">
                <div class="action-buttons">
                  <a
                    class="btn btn-primary btn-sm btn-block"
                    href="{{ url_for('file_detail', domain_id=result.domain_id, relative_path=row.relative_path, replay_path_input=result.path_input or '', replay_recursive=('1' if result.recursive else '0'), replay_sources=result.source_ids|join(',')) }}"
                  >Compare</a>
                  {% if row.gold_source_id %}
                    {% if row.available_source_ids %}
                      <a
                        class="btn btn-secondary btn-sm btn-block"
                        href="{{ url_for('gold_form', domain_id=result.domain_id, relative_path=row.relative_path, mode='change', allowed_ids=row.available_source_ids|join(','), replay_domain_id=result.domain_id, replay_path_input=result.path_input or '', replay_recursive=('1' if result.recursive else '0'), replay_sources=result.source_ids|join(','), current_gold=row.gold_source_id) }}"
                      >Change Gold</a>
                    {% endif %}
                    <form method="post" action="{{ url_for('gold_remove') }}" class="inline-form">
                      <input type="hidden" name="domain_id" value="{{ result.domain_id }}">
                      <input type="hidden" name="relative_path" value="{{ row.relative_path }}">
                      <input type="hidden" name="replay_domain_id" value="{{ result.domain_id }}">
                      <input type="hidden" name="replay_path_input" value="{{ result.path_input or '' }}">
                      <input type="hidden" name="replay_recursive" value="{{ '1' if result.recursive else '0' }}">
                      {% for sid in result.source_ids %}
                        <input type="hidden" name="replay_source_id" value="{{ sid }}">
                      {% endfor %}
                      <button type="submit" class="btn btn-secondary btn-sm btn-block">Remove Gold</button>
                    </form>
                  {% elif row.available_source_ids %}
                    <a
                      class="btn btn-secondary btn-sm btn-block"
                      href="{{ url_for('gold_form', domain_id=result.domain_id, relative_path=row.relative_path, mode='set', allowed_ids=row.available_source_ids|join(','), replay_domain_id=result.domain_id, replay_path_input=result.path_input or '', replay_recursive=('1' if result.recursive else '0'), replay_sources=result.source_ids|join(',')) }}"
                    >Set Gold</a>
                  {% endif %}
                </div>
              </td>
            </tr>
          {% endfor %}
        </tbody>
      </table>
    </div>
  </div>
{% endif %}
{% endblock %}

  <ul style="margin: 0; padding-left: 1.25rem;">
    {% for r in rollback_results %}
      <li><code>{{ r.step }}</code> — id <strong>{{ r.id }}</strong> — <strong>{{ r.status }}</strong>{% if r.error %} ({{ r.error }}){% endif %}</li>
    {% endfor %}
  </ul>
  {% else %}
  <p class="page-description">No per-step rollback entries were stored.</p>
  {% endif %}
  {% endif %}

  {% if has_rollback_stack and rollback_stack_entries %}
  <h2 class="page-title" style="font-size: 1.1rem; margin-top: 1.5rem;">
    {% if rollback_executed %}Rollback stack (audit){% else %}Rollback stack (planned){% endif %}
  </h2>
  <p class="page-description">{% if rollback_executed %}Kept for audit after rollback.{% else %}Order: resource row first, then license server.{% endif %}</p>
  <ul style="margin: 0; padding-left: 1.25rem;">
    {% for entry in rollback_stack_entries %}
      <li><code>{{ entry.type }}</code> — {{ entry.table }} id <strong>{{ entry.id }}</strong></li>
    {% endfor %}
  </ul>
  {% endif %}

  <h2 class="page-title" style="font-size: 1.1rem; margin-top: 1.5rem;">Collected inputs</h2>
  <pre class="operation-pre">{{ operation.inputs | tojson(indent=2) }}</pre>

{% macro status_label(s) -%}

{%- elif s == 'in_progress' -%}In progress
{%- elif s == 'published' -%}Published
{%- elif s == 'rolled_back' -%}Rolled back
{%- elif s == 'applied' -%}Applied
{%- elif s == 'reused' -%}Reused (satisfied)
{%- else -%}{{ s }}
{%- endif -%}
{%- endmacro %}

  .workspace-status--table.workspace-status--rolled_back { background: #fecaca; color: #7f1d1d; }

  .tw-lead { margin: 0.75rem 0; padding: 0.65rem 0.85rem; border-radius: 6px; background: #f3f4f6; border: 1px solid rgba(0,0,0,0.06); }
  .tw-lead--preview { background: #dbeafe; border-color: #93c5fd; }
  .tw-lead--satisfied { background: #d1fae5; border-color: #6ee7b7; }

{% if twf %}
